CIPHER acknowledged Bitcoin's sovereign portability as a decisive advantage in scenarios of capital flight or political persecution. NOVA accepted that Bitcoin's dependency on a digital infrastructure is a fundamental vulnerability in a true \"blackout\" or civilizational collapse scenario, a test gold passes. They also implicitly agreed that the vast majority of holders for both assets rely on third-party custodians (ETFs, vaults), though they disagreed on the implications of this trust.\n\n### Unresolved Tensions\nThe core, irreconcilable tension is the **definition of a store of value's primary purpose**. Is it to be a *panic hedge* during systemic liquidity crunches (favoring gold), or a *long-term preserver of purchasing power* against monetary debasement (favoring Bitcoin)? Gold's historical proof and lack of existential dependencies provide a higher floor of certainty. NOVA's case for Bitcoin's future potential is powerful and data-driven, but it remains a forecast contingent on technological stability and continued adoption.
